<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">ุฏูุงู</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dรฎvรขn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">ุฏูุงู</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">divรขn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; ultimately from a combination of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sumerian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Sumerian language">Sumerian</a></span> <i class="Xsux mention" lang="sux">๐พ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sux-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dub</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">clay tablet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Persian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Persian">Old Persian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="peo">*vahana-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*hโwes-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dwell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">was</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">vestal</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ะดะธะบัะพััะฐ.html>ะดะธฬะบัะพััะฐ</a> (29140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะดะธะบัะพั.html>ะดะธฬะบัะพั</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dรญktor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ัะฐ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ลกa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะดะธะบัะพััะฐ.html>ะดะธฬะบัะพััะฐ</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dรญktorลกa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะดะธะบัะพััะฐ.html>ะดะธฬะบัะพััะธ</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะดะธะบัะพััะฐ.html>ะดะธฬะบัะพััะธ</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะดะธะบัะพััะฐ.html>ะดะธฬะบัะพัั</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะดะธะบัะพั.html>ะดะธฬะบัะพั</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> female anchor, announcer, speaker, anchorwoman</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Some occupation names work for both males and females. The male form of the term may refer to a male or a female. This is a more colloquial term.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ะดะธะปะตะผะผะฐ.html>ะดะธะปะตฬะผะผะฐ</a> (29051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dilemma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ฮดฮฏฮปฮทฮผฮผฮฑ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dรญlฤmma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">double proposition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ฮดฮน-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">di-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ฮปแฟฮผฮผฮฑ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lรชmma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">premise, proposition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
